Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageActs contact form
URLhttps://www.actsretirement.org/visit-acts/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score1170
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1170, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 220. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 200. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 88

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 86 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 74

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 72 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 74

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 20 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test link-name, score 15 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 16 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 24 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_A_HasText, score 20 (Hyperlink has no text description)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 24 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 8 (Link has no text inside it)
  • Package tenon, test 91, score 16 (Link has a background image but no text inside it)

  • Package wave, test e:label_missing, score 20 (form element has no label)
